      <tr>
        <td id="L94" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="94"></td>
        <td id="LC94" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">1.1 Standardized APMs</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L95" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="95"></td>
        <td id="LC95" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">===============================================================================</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L96" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="96"></td>
        <td id="LC96" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L97" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="97"></td>
        <td id="LC97" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This section defines a standardized Actions-Per-Minute(APM) value.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L98" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="98"></td>
        <td id="LC98" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">With it we hope to make APM values more comparable inbetween all current and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L99" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="99"></td>
        <td id="LC99" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">future replay tools out there and coming. Please use it in your tool too :D</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L100" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="100"></td>
        <td id="LC100" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L101" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="101"></td>
        <td id="LC101" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The main goal is an easy-to-implement algorithm. This way even simple replay</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L102" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="102"></td>
        <td id="LC102" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">tools should have no difficulties at all to calculate it.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L103" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="103"></td>
        <td id="LC103" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L104" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="104"></td>
        <td id="LC104" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Basic rules:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L105" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="105"></td>
        <td id="LC105" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Only count in-game actions (no map-signals, no chat).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L106" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="106"></td>
        <td id="LC106" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Every counted action increments the player action counter by one.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L107" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="107"></td>
        <td id="LC107" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Do not filter out any player action.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L108" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="108"></td>
        <td id="LC108" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o APM = numbers of actions of a player / time this player played.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L109" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="109"></td>
        <td id="LC109" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L110" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="110"></td>
        <td id="LC110" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Accordingly all actions in section 2.0 are marked in the headline:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L111" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="111"></td>
        <td id="LC111" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> [APM+] = Action is counted.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L112" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="112"></td>
        <td id="LC112" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> [APM?] = Special, please read the notes on this action (0x16, 0x19).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L113" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="113"></td>
        <td id="LC113" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> [APM-] = Action is not counted.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L114" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="114"></td>
        <td id="LC114" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L115" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="115"></td>
        <td id="LC115" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Additionally you have to pay attention to the pause/unpause actions in order to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L116" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="116"></td>
        <td id="LC116" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">determine the played time correctly:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L117" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="117"></td>
        <td id="LC117" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> Pause game (action 0x01):</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L118" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="118"></td>
        <td id="LC118" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   o Stop the time at the first occurence of this action</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L119" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="119"></td>
        <td id="LC119" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     (there might be multiple ones).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L120" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="120"></td>
        <td id="LC120" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   o The pause action itself is not counted.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L121" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="121"></td>
        <td id="LC121" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   o Do NOT stop counting the actions within a pause</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L122" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="122"></td>
        <td id="LC122" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     (but skip actions like map signals as usual).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L123" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="123"></td>
        <td id="LC123" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> Resume game (action 0x02):</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L124" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="124"></td>
        <td id="LC124" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   o Resume counting the time at first occurence of this action</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L125" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="125"></td>
        <td id="LC125" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">     (there might be multiple ones).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L126" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="126"></td>
        <td id="LC126" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   o Do not count this action itself.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L127" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="127"></td>
        <td id="LC127" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L128" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="128"></td>
        <td id="LC128" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Due to this simple method there are the following inadequacies:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L129" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="129"></td>
        <td id="LC129" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Cancelling a unit/building by pressing Escape key will be counted twice</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L130" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="130"></td>
        <td id="LC130" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   (Action 0x61 + Action 0x10 with unitid=0x08000D00).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L131" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="131"></td>
        <td id="LC131" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Map signal are uncounted. They are no real in-game actions and can very</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L132" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="132"></td>
        <td id="LC132" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   easily abused to increase the APM value.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L133" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="133"></td>
        <td id="LC133" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o No &#39;tab&#39; action are counted (since patch 1.14b).</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L134" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="134"></td>
        <td id="LC134" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   (Prior to patch 1.14b only the last action of a complete cycle through all</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L135" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="135"></td>
        <td id="LC135" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    subgroups was not counted.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L136" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="136"></td>
        <td id="LC136" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L137" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="137"></td>
        <td id="LC137" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Keep in mind that for the APM value it is not important, which consequences</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L138" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="138"></td>
        <td id="LC138" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">within the game an action has. It is only significant *how often* it is used.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L139" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="139"></td>
        <td id="LC139" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If a player executes a specific action once every minute, it only results in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L140" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="140"></td>
        <td id="LC140" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a 1 APM difference at the end.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L141" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="141"></td>
        <td id="LC141" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Do you really need a APM precision better than say ±5 APMs ?</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L142" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="142"></td>

        <td id="LC873" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Stringencoded ID&#39;s contain four valid characters.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L874" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="874"></td>
        <td id="LC874" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> o Alphanumeric ID&#39;s have always the format: ?? ?? 0D 00</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L954" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="954"></td>
        <td id="LC954" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Numeric ItemID&#39;s are only used on EXECUTION of abilities/spells.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L955" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="955"></td>
        <td id="LC955" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(e.g. hero spells, unit spells, autocast on/off)</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1356" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1356"></td>

        <td id="LC1357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">object in &#39;change selection&#39; actions or for denoting target objects.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L1358" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="1358"></td>
